M_virus_action_20 = {
	available = {
	OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
		tooltip = M_virus_action_20_1
			has_war = no		
		}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
		tooltip = M_virus_action_20_2
			has_country_flag = PRC_AIMAO_SSMAO		
		}
	}
	}
	activation = {
			has_war = yes	
	}
	is_good = no
	selectable_mission = no
	fire_only_once = yes
	days_mission_timeout = 720
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = PRC_AIMAO_SSMAO	}	
				}
			country_event = {
				id = PRC_MAO.175
			}
			}
	}
	timeout_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = PRC_MAO.174
			}
	}
}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 25
		}
		allowed = {
			original_tag = HKN
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				any_controlled_state = {

				}
			}
			any_controlled_state = {

			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
				any_controlled_state = {
					is_capital = no
				}
			}
		}

		 fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			NOT = {has_country_flag = M_virus_action_9_flag}
			NOT = {PRC = {has_completed_focus = PRC_rumaojiehe_87}}
			tag = HKN
			has_completed_focus = HKZ_ZOM_9
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
					set_country_flag = M_virus_action_9_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
					clr_country_flag = M_virus_action_9_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						any_controlled_state = {
